<pb n="001"/>
ṛjuvimalā pañcikā
<q>śālikanāthamiśrakṛtā</q>
(bṛhatīvyākhyā)
<lg><l>sṛ1ṣṭāvidyāniśādhvaṃsinibandhamayavāsaram ।</l>
<l>ujjāsitajagajjāḍyaṃ namasyāmaḥ prabhākaram ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>prabhākaramayīṃ dṛṣṭiṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadhataṃ sadā ।</l>
<l>vāmadarśanatāpannacandraṃ vande'parājitam ।। 2 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>prabhākaragurorbhāvama2tigambhīrabhāṣiṇaḥ ।</l>
<l>añjasā vyañjayiṣyantī pañcikā3 kriyate mayā ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>upanyāsanirāsābhyāṃ vyāsenaiṣā vidūṣitā ।</l>
<l>vyākhyā prācāṃ nibandhṝṇāmiti nāhamadūduṣam ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>

prayojanaṃ darśayati---<q>loka ityādibhāṣyasyetyādinā</q> । sarvasūtrasthasarvapadaviṣayaṃ

ityatra kvacit <quote>“ujjhāsita”</quote> iti dṛśyate;

sādhanamupāyaḥ, sādhyatvopāyatve ca bhinne; kiṃ tu kleśātmakaṃ karmāpekṣitopāyatayā

vibhāgamuttaradeśena saṃyogaṃ cārabhata ityubhayamupapannam । na ca calati---iti
vartamānāvabodha ekakriyākṣaṇābhiprāyeṇa, kṣaṇasya paurvāparyābhāvāt । tasmātkriyākṣa-

pratītiḥ । taduktam---</p>

<lg><l><quote>“yadā tvādyaparispanda1prabhṛtyā phalalābhataḥ ।</l>
<l>kriyā pūrvāparībhūtā lakṣyate vartate tadā”</quote> ।। iti ।</l></lg>
<p>na ca karmahotereva saṃyogavibhāgodayaḥ । tathā hi---ātmaśarīrasaṃyogā-
dātmāśritaprayatnānugṛhītātpādahastādiṣu karmeṣyate । taduktam---<quote>“ātmaśarīra-
saṃyogaprayatnābhyāṃ haste karma”</quote>---iti । saṃyogaśca saṃyoginyeva kārya-
mārabhate yathāvayavinabhavayavasaṃyogaḥ । saṃyogavibhāgau ca na kevalamāśraya-
samavetau, anāśraye'pi deśe samavāyāt । tenātmasaṃyogātiriktamaparaṃ karmānumīyate । na
ca tatrāyaṃ niyamo dṛṣṭaḥ---svāśraya eva phalamārabhate---iti, tasyāpūrvatvāt; tenānumeya-
tve'pi na kaściddoṣaḥ । pratyakṣatvaṃ tu pratītiviruddham; na hi saṃyogavibhāgātiriktaṃ
nipuṇamapi nirūpayadbhiraparaṃ vastūpalabhyate । taduktam---<quote>“na hi te pratyakṣe”</quote>
iti । kimarthaṃ tarhi---<quote>“devadattasya gatipūrvikāṃ deśāntaraprāptimupalabhyāditye'pi
gatismaraṇam”</quote> ityuktam ? devadatte'pyanumeyatvāt । ucyate---devadatte
tāvadātmasaṃyogātirekiṇyanu2mite tatsāmānyādāditye'pi gatirevānumīyate, devadatte
deśāntaraprāptestatkāraṇatvena niścitatvāt । etaduktaṃ bhavati---sarvatra cetane
vācetane vā gatireva deśāntaraprāptau nimittamiti । <q>ataḥ sāmānyamātraparyavasāyya6-
pyanumānamasti</q> । <q>darśitaṃ ca devadattasya gatipūrvikāmiti</q> ।</p>
<p>idānīṃ lakṣaṇābhidhānaprayojanaṃ pṛcchati---<q>kaḥ pu4naranumāne vyabhi-

arthāparipūrteḥ śabdo'pyaparipūrṇaḥ iti cet, bhavatvevam; 2yannibandhanā hi

pūrṇatā syāt । tasmādaparipūrṇatve'pi śabdasya artha eva kalpanīyaḥ । na cārthānu-
papattau śabdasyānupapattiḥ, bhinnatvācchabdārthayoḥ । athocyeta---arthānupapattau prame-
yābhāve śabdasya pramāṇatāpyanupapannaiva---iti; evamapi pramāṇatānupapannā syāt,
na śabdaḥ । na ca pramāṇatā pṛthaganupapannā, kiṃ tu arthānupapattyaiva; evaṃ cenmūla-
bhūtārthānupapattirevārthāpattyupasthāpikāstu । api ca pramāṇatāpi kenacidarthena vinā
prameyābhāvaśaṅkayānupapannā, na śabdābhāvena, yena śabdaṃ kalpayedityalamativicā-
reṇa । dūramantaritā vayaṃ prakṛtamanusarāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>ta3trottaram---<q>abhidhānāntaramevedamupalabdhervācakam</q> । asyārthaḥ---dṛṣṭa-
śabdamātreṇa na sarvaparigrahaḥ, kiṃ tu śrutaśabdasahitena; tena śrutagrahaṇaṃ nānarthakam ।
kathaṃ punaḥ śrutagrahaṇasahitena dṛṣṭaśabdenopalabdhatocyate ? śrūyatām-dṛṣṭaśabdena yadya-
pyupalabdhamātramucyate, tathāpi śrutaśabdasannidhānāt gobalīvardanyāyena śabdapramitavya-
tiriktamucyate । nanvetasya gobalīvardanyāyasyāśrayaṇe kiṃ prayojanam ? ucyate---
laukikā vayam; lokaścetyamapi vyavaharamāṇo dṛśyate; na ca loke paryanuyogāvakāśo'-
sti, anāditvāt । ata idamuktamabhidhānāntaramevedaṃ lokapratītamupalabdhervācakamiti ।।</p>
<p>ityarthāpattiprakaraṇam ।।</p>

bdhikāraṇaṃ pramāṇāntaraṃ yasya yāgena saha paśūnāṃ sādhyasādhanabhāvasya sa vidyamā-

paśukāmaḥ”</quote> ityādi । pha1lasādhanatānibandhanā kāryataiva liṅādibhirabhidhīyate iti ।
<q>kātra vidyamānopalambhanatā ? kriyānantaraphalabhāvitā</q> kriyānantaraṃ phalasya bhavana-
śīlatā । <q>dṛṣṭārthatvācca vṛṣṭyādeḥ</q> । śuṣyatsu vrīhyādiṣu vṛṣṭyādi kāmyamānamanantara-
phalabhāvitayaivāvaga2myata ityanayā'pi yuktyānantarabhāvitā yuktā । śakyate cānantara-
phalabhāvitayā karmaṇaḥ pramāṇāntaragamyatāsya sādhyasādhanabhāvātmakavastuno vak‍tumu-
ktena nyāyena । saṃbhavati ca pramāṇāntaraviṣayatve phalanibandhanayāgakartavyatāviṣa-
yatve, ko hi nāmādṛṣṭaṃ svātantryaṃ kalpayituṃ loke śabdasya kṣamaḥ ? tasmānniyogaḥ
praiṣādyarthatulya eva; yathā praiṣādiṣu laukikeṣu vaidikeṣu ca niyogaḥ, sa ca pramāṇā-
ntarapūrvakaḥ, tathā vidhyuddeśagato'pīti pratipattavyam । yadidamuktasmābhiḥ tadidam
<quote>‘kutaḥ’</quote> ityasya praśnasya <quote>‘vidyamānopalambhanatvāt’</quote> ityuttaraṃ dattaṃ bhāṣye । <q>nanvevaṃ
granthe vyākhyāyamāne <quote>“paśavo nopalabhyante”</quote> ityādiranarthako granthaḥ</q> ।
upalabhyantāṃ paśavo mā vopalabhyantām, sarvathā pramāṇāntarasāpekṣaṃ śābdamitye-

nirākriyate । kena kāreṇana nirākriyata ityetannopapadyata ityanena kāraṇenetyarthaḥ ।
kathaṃ punaḥ saṃśleṣasambandhanirākaraṇenedam <quote>‘śabdādartho'vagamyate’</quote> iti nirākṛtaṃ bhavati ?
na hyanyasmin nirākṛte'nyannirākṛtaṃ bhavatītyabhiprāyaḥ । <q>bhavatīti</q> । uttaram ।
bhavati nirākṛtamityarthaḥ । kutaḥ ? śabdādarthajñānaṃ hi kārya kenacitkāraṇena; tatra
tāvanna śabdādeva kevalādidaṃ kāryamutpadyata iti śakyate vaktuṃ cakṣurādīnāmiva yathā
cakṣurādīnāṃ kāryaṃ cakṣurādibhya evotpadyate, tathedamapīti na1 । kasmāt ?
prathamaśravaṇādapratīteḥ । ekagranthenāha---evaṃ tarhi evaṃ ca sati svarūpamevaśabdasya
arthajñāne na kāraṇam yathā dhūmādīnāṃ na svarūpamevāgnyādyavagatau kāraṇam ।

bhūtasambandhāntaranirākaraṇena kāryabhūtā vācyavācakataiva nirākṛtā bhavati ।

cchabdatvamevāṅgīkriyate nimittam ? atrottaram---<q>sāmānyaviśeṣaviṣaya-

viśeṣaṇamupāttam ; na hi jvālānāṃ bhedakaṃ kiñcidavabudhyate । ekabuddhirapi tatra
bhedāgrahaṇanibandhaneti śabdādhikaraṇe vakṣyāmaḥ । <q>na ca gakārādiṣu eka-

<p><quote>“nanvākṛtiḥ sādhyāsti vā na vā”</quote> iti bhāṣyamākṛtisadbhāvamākṣipati ;

gran‍tho varṇanīyaḥ । sa tu tadbha‍ūtādhikaraṇe svayameva bhāṣyakāreṇaiva varṇita
<quote>“padārthapratipattidvāreṇaiva padānāṃ vākyārthapratipādakatvam”</quote> iti vadatā; tena
nimittabhūtākṛtyarthatoktā । etaccottaratrāpi ṭīkākāreṇoktam । saṃprati nirākṛtapakṣa
ekadeśyeva siddhāntinaṃ paryanuyuṅkte---<q>kastarhyanaikāntikaparihāra iti</q> । uttaraṃ
dadāti---<q>nimittābhiprāyaṃ taducyate; apratipannanimittaḥ prathamaśrutānna
pratipadyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---nimittaṃ vākyārthapratipādane padārthātmakamabhipretyocyate
<quote>“prathamaśrutaḥ kiṃ na pratyāyayati”</quote> iti । etaduktaṃ bhavati---prathamaśrutaṃ padaṃ
nimittabhūtaṃ padārtha na pratipādayati; apratipannanimittaśca prathamaśrutātpadādvākyā-
rthamapi na pratipadyata iti siddhaṃ vede'pi prathamaśrutasyāpratipādakatvam । tasmā-
cchabdādanyannimittāntaraṃ vākyārthapratipatterityabhiprāyaḥ । nanvevaṃ yadi sarvapadānyeva
vākyārthapratipattau nimittabhūtāni tadā vaiyākaraṇadarśanamaṅgīkṛtam---sarvaṃ padajātaṃ
militvā vākyārthaṃ pratipādayatīti, tatra kālpanika eva vibhāga iti । tadane-
nābhiprāyeṇāha---<q>kaḥ punarvācakanimittayorbheda iti</q> । uttaram---idamarthameva
hi bhedakathanārthameva hi ta dbha‍ūtādhikaraṇamārabhyate । tatredamucyate---nimittapakṣe
padāni svārtheṣvanviteṣu vyāpriyamāṇāni vākyārthapratipattimupajanayanti, na punaḥ
pratyastamitapadavibhāgamanavayavameva vākyārthaṃ vaktīti । evaṃ ca kathyamāne kathita eva
vācakanimittayorbheda ityalaṃ prapañcena; tadbha‍ūtādhikaraṇa eva prapañco bhaviṣyati ।
﻿<pb n="190"/>
<q><quote>“na, siddhavadupadeśāt”</quote></q> । atra ca sūtre <quote>‘upadeśaḥ’</quote> iti prathamāntaṃ pañcamya
ntatayā vipariṇamayya siddhavaditi cādhyāhṛtya bhāṣyakāreṇedamuktam । asyārthaḥ---
siddhavadidaṃ sambandhasyāpauruṣeyatvaṃ siddhamityarthaḥ । upadeśāt vṛddhopadeśāt,
ekena vṛddhenāparasmai vṛddhāyānuṣṭhānopadeśe pārśvasthasya sambandhagrahaṇasaṃskāra
mātrādevārthapratītyupapatteḥ sambandhṛkalpanānupapattiḥ । tamimamasyārthamabuddhvā
pṛcchati---<q>kimidaṃ siddhavadupadeśāditi । idamidam</q>---nātra sambandhasya
kartā <q>śakyate kalpayitumiti, vṛddhavyavāharasyānāditvāt । ata
autpattikaḥ sambandha iti siddham</q> । yadi vṛddhavyavahāro'nādirna
syāt, tadā prathamavṛddhayoḥ sambandhagrahaṇopāyābhāvācchabdaprayogārthapratītī
na syātām; tadabhāvācca vṛddhavyavahārāpravṛttāvapareṣāmapi sambandhāgrahaṇe tathaiva
prayogapratītī vicchidyeyātām; anādistu vṛddhavyavahāraḥ, puruṣāntara-
pūrvakatvātpuruṣāntarotpatteḥ । yathā khalvadyatanāḥ puruṣāḥ puruṣāntarapūrvakāḥ
tathā prācyā apīti ।</p>
<p>atra kecidarthavādagatasṛṣṭipralayaśrutyupanipātamātropajātaśraddhātiśayavi-

﻿<pb n="191"/>

pauruṣeyatvaṃ sāpekṣatvāpādakamautpattikasambandhābhidhānena nirastam । loke tu
svātantryādarśanena śabdasya yā pramāṇāntaragocaraikaviṣayatvaśaṅkā, sā
nirākriyate । autpattike'pi sambandhe viṣayāntaraṃ svatantraṃ śabdasyetyayaṃ
viveko'nukta iva pratibhāti, tadvivekāyedaṃ codyaṃ punarupanyasyate । <quote>“karma-
kāle phalādarśanātkālāntare ca karmābhāvāt”</quote> ityanena bhāṣyaṃ paṭhitvākṣi-
﻿<pb n="200"/>
pati । nanu cānena viṣayāntaravivekāyopanyastena bhāṣyeṇa kiṃ prayojanam ?
yasmāt <q>viṣayāntarābhāvāt pramāṇāntaraviṣayatayā ca sāpekṣatvāttadabhāve
cāprāmāṇyaṃ darśitam</q> । śabdasya pramāṇāntarāvedyaviṣayatvābhāvātpramāṇāntara-
grāhyarthaviṣayatayā ca pramāṇāntarasāpekṣatvātpramāṇāntarābhāve cāprāmāṇyaṃ
darśitaṃ citrākṣepe, ihāpi tadevānena bhāṣyeṇoktamiti । <q>kiṃ punastat
yadanuktamiva pratibhāti</q> ? yadanena bhāṣyeṇocyate । samādhatte---<q>idaṃ tat;
pramāṇāntaraviṣayatve hyanenedamityasmin sati niyogaḥ । tatra cānupalabdhe
sphuṭamevāprāmāṇyam</q> iti prāguktameva । <q>na cāsminnarthe saṃbhavati niyogādeva
niyogasiddhiriti śakyate kalpayitum</q> । idaṃ tadanuktamuktamanena
bhāṣyeṇeti sambandhaḥ asyārthaḥ---yadyapi karmānantaraṃ phalaṃ na sidhyati,
kālāntare ca nāsti karma, tathāpi niyogādeva kālāntare phalaṃ bhaviṣyatīti;
tadanena parihriyate । yasmādasminnarthe pramāṇāntaraviṣayātmake saṃbhavati
niyogādeva phalasiddhiriti na śakyate kalpayitum, niyogasya tadānīmapramāṇa-
katvāt; niyogo hi pramāṇāntarāvedyasvarūpaḥ; kathaṃ pramāṇāntarasāpekṣaśabda-
prameyaḥ syāt ? tasmāt karmānantaraṃ phalādarśanāt kālāntare ca
karmābhāvānnāsti pramāṇaṃ paśuphaleṣṭiriti । tasmādanupalabdhe sphuṭamaprāmāṇyaṃ
codanāyā iti । <q>tadidānīṃ nirākriyate---syādetadevaṃ yadyautpattikatā
na syāt; sādhitā cāsau</q> । yadyautpattikaḥ sambandhaḥ, tataḥ <q>kim ? idaṃ</q>
<pb n="201"/>
<q>tataḥ</q> । nānena karmaṇedaṃ phalaṃ sidhyatītyamumarthamapekṣate niyogaḥ । asyā-
bhiprāyaḥ---yadi hi pauruṣeyaḥ sambandhaḥ syāt, tadā balātpauruṣeyatā
codanāyā āpadyeta; tathā ca sati pramāṇāntaraviṣayatvāpatteḥ sādhyasādhanabhāvā-
pekṣa eva niyogārthaḥ syāt; sādhite tvapauruṣeye sambandhe svātantryāvirodhā-
nnāprāmāṇyaṃ śakyate vaditum । yattūktam---loke svātantryaṃ na pratīyata
iti, tatrāha---<q>pramāṇāntarasamadhigamye'pi hi laukike'rthe naiva niyogasya
sādhyasādhanasidhyapekṣāvasīyate</q> । asyārthaḥ---pravṛttidarśanena liṅādīnāṃ
kāryārthapratipādakatvaṃ tāvadavagamyate loke; tathā vyutpannāste svārthābhidhāne
na pramāṇāntaramapekṣante । ato yadyapi vaktā pramāṇāntarapratītāmeva kāryatāṃ
vivakṣati, tathāpi śabdaḥ svasāmarthyenaiva tāṃ pratipādayati; tena vede'pi
na sādhyasādhanāvagamapūrvako liṅādibhirartho'bhidhīyate । niyogaśabdena cātra
liṅādirabhipretaḥ । darśitaṃ ca bhāṣye---<quote>“ācāryacoditaḥ karomīti hi
dṛśyate”</quote>, na anenāsya siddhiriti । etaduktaṃ bhavati---yataḥ pratipattā
kāryameva pratipadyānutiṣṭhati, na punaḥ sādhyasādhanabhāvam; ataḥ kurvāṇa
āpṛṣṭaḥ <quote>‘ācāryacodito'hamācāryeṇa kāryaṃ bodhayitvā preritaḥ karomi’</quote>
iti vyapadiśati, na sādhyasādhanabhāvāgavamam । yadi pauruṣeye'pi vākye
pratipattā nirapekṣameva kāryaṃ budhyate, tadā kimiti tarhi puruṣāpekṣā sambandhasya
nirākriyate ? bhavatu pauruṣeyaḥ sambandho vedāśca pauruṣeyāḥ, tathāpi nirapekṣārthaprati-
pādakatayā prāmāṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati । atrottaram---<q>kāraṇadoṣasambhāvanānirākaraṇāya
nirākriyate, na punarātmasaṃvittau</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadi pauruṣeyatvaṃ na nirākriyeta,
tadotpannāpi kāryapratītiḥ kāraṇadoṣānmithyā syāt; pramāṇapratītaṃ hi svayamarthaṃ
puruṣaḥ parasmai pratipādayati । tatra ca pauruṣeyasya vacanasya kāryasya kāraṇā-
﻿<pb n="202"/>
numāpakatā । yadi ca vedānāṃ pauruṣeyatā syāt, tadā pramāṇāntareṇa vedārthaṃ
pratītya puruṣeṇopadeśaḥ kāryaḥ; na ca pramāṇāntaramastīti kāraṇadoṣā-
dutpannāpi pratītirmithyā syāt; <quote>‘caityaṃ vandeta svargakāmaḥ’</quote> <quote>‘saṅghāya bhaktaṃ dadyāt
svargakāmaḥ’</quote> itivat; na punarātmasaṃvittau pramātuḥ svayaṃ pratipattau sāpekṣatā
bhavatītyevamarthaṃ nirākriyate । upasaṃharati---<q>tasmāt svātantryaṃ niyogasyetya-
nena vivekaḥ pradarśyate</q> । yadi svātantryaṃ niyogasya, na1 tarhi svargayāgayoḥ sādhya-
sādhanabhāvāvagamaḥ pratīyate; viṣayaniyojyamātrāvacchinno hi niyogaḥ pratipādyeta
nityādhikāravadityatrāha---<q>puruṣaṃ hi niyuñjānaḥ sādhyasiddhimavagamayati</q> ।
etacca ṣaṣṭhe sayuktikaṃ vakṣyati । tadāha---<q>iti ṣaṣṭhe pratipādayiṣyatīti</q> ।
yadyapi svātantryeṇa kāryaṃ liṅādiravagamayati; <q>kimevaṃ satyanantarānupalabdhirnirastā
bhavati</q> ? kāmādhikāre hi phalasiddhiparyanto vākyārthaḥ; phalaṃ caitadanantaraṃ na
dṛśyate tadā pramāṇāntaraviparyayādaprāmāṇyamāpādayantī kimanantarānupalabdhi-
rnirastā bhavati ? <q>bāḍhaṃ nirastā</q> । na prāmāṇyamāpādayituṃ kṣamā । kasmā-
dityāha---<q>na hyetasmin pakṣe kriyāśaktinirūpaṇāt sādhyasiddhiḥ । kiṃ
tarhi ? niyogārthavaśāt</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadi hi kriyāśaktinirūpaṇāt
sādhyasiddhiḥ, tadānantarameva phalena bhavitavyamiti śās‍trārthaḥ syāt; na cāsmin
pakṣe svātantryeṇa kāryābhidhānapakṣe <quote>‘yasmādiyaṃ kriyā phalaṃ sādhayituṃ śaknoti,
tasmātkāryaphalasiddhiścātaḥ’</quote> ityevaṃ kriyāśaktiṃ nirūpya sādhyasiddhiḥ । kiṃ tarhi ?
yasmātkāmī kāryaṃ bodhyate, tasmātkāryaṃ phalamiti । na ca kṣaṇabhaṅgurāṃ kriyāṃ
<note>1. Omitted na. ka. ga.</note>
﻿<pb n="203"/>
niyatadehāntarabhogyasvargasādhanāśaktāṃ svargakāmaḥ kāryatayā bodbha‍umalamityapūrvaṃ
kālāntarāvasthāyiphalasiddhisamarthaṃ liṅādayaḥ kāryatayā bodhayantīti tasya
sthās‍nutayā kālāntare'pi phalasādhanatvāvirodhāt; tasmādyāgādasyāpūrvasiddhi-
vyavadhānena phalasiddhirityetāvadavagamyate; nānantaraṃ vyavahitaṃ veti । <q>taccāna-
pekṣatvaṃ yatrataḥ pratipāditam</q> । yattatprāmāṇyāpādakam <quote>‘anenedaṃ sidhyati’</quote> ityeta-
darthānapekṣatvam, tacca yatrataḥ sādhitamapauruṣeyatvapratipādanena । <q>kimidaṃ <quote>“yadi
pañcaiva pramāṇyānyabhaviṣyan”</quote> iti</q> ? śabdātirekipramāṇapañcakopanyāso na
yuktaḥ, pramāṇapañcakāṅgīkārāt । <q>idamevedamiti</q> । na pañcasaṃkhyāparikīrtana-
manupapannam । punarākṣepaka āha---<q>nanūktamabhāvo'pi pramāṇābhāva iti</q> ।
pramāṇābhāvo'bhāva ityuktam, tena pañcapramāṇaniyamānnedamupapannamiti । sāvaṣṭambhaṃ
samarthayitāha---<q>kimato yadyevam</q> ? akṣeptaivāha---<q>etadato bhavati---pañca
pramāṇānīti nopapadyate</q> । samādhātāha---<q>śakyate vā caturbhirnāstīti
vaktum</q> ? kākvā na śakyata ityāha । śabdavyatiriktaiścaturbhiḥ pramāṇairnāstīti
śabdaprayogātmako vyavahāraḥ pravartayituṃ na śakyate । ākṣeptāha---<q>pramāṇaṃ
tarhyabhāvaḥ</q> । atra samādhātā granthavirodhaṃ tāvadāha---<q>pramāṇaṃ vā pramāṇā-
bhāva iti śakyate vaktum</q> ? atrāpi kākvā na śakyata ityuktam । yadi
pramāṇāntaramabhāvaḥ syāt, pramāṇābhāva iti kathaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇocyate ?
yuktyāpyabhāvasya pramāṇāntaratvaṃ nāstītyāha---<q>abhāvasya prāmāṇyeṃ pratyakṣādi</q>-
﻿<pb n="204"/>
<q>viṣayāpekṣitā viṣaye</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadyabhāvaḥ pramāṇaṃ tadā pratyakṣādi-
paricchinnātiriktaviṣayāntarānupapatteḥ sāpekṣatā abhāvasya syāt । tathā hi---
na tāvat pratyakṣeṇa bhūtalaṃ ghāṭādisadbhāve sātireki svarūpameva gabhyaṃ <quote>‘nāsti’</quote>
iti pratyetavyam; kintu dṛśye'pi ghaṭādau svarūpamātreṇopalabdhamiti; tena
sāpekṣatā viṣaye paricchedye'bhāvasya tadatiriktaviṣayāntarābhavāt । yacca
svātantryeṇa viṣayaṃ nopasthāpayati, na tatpramāṇāntaram । <q>ataḥ pramāṇāntara-
pramitaviṣayāvacchedakatayaivāsya lakṣaṇābhidhānam</q> । pramāṇānāṃ pratyakṣādīnāṃ
viṣayasyāvacchedakatayā <quote>‘ayameva’</quote> ityevaṃ niścāyakatayāsya lakṣaṇam, na punaḥ
pramāṇāntaratayā । anena lakṣaṇagranthavirodhaḥ parihṛtaḥ । saṃpratyākṣepaṃ pariharati---
<q>vyavahārānyatvaṃ tu saṃpratipannameva</q> । nāstīti vyapadeśasya niḥśaṅkagamanā-
dilakṣaṇasya vyavahārasyānyatvaṃ saṃpratipannameva saṃmatameva । <q>vyavahārasiddha‍yarthaścā-
yamupanyāsaḥ, na pramāṇasvarūpasiddha‍yarthaḥ</q> । śabdenāpi vyavahāraḥ kartavya
ityevamarthamupanyastam---syādetadevam yadi pañcaiva pramāṇānyabhaviṣyanniti ।
tenāyamartho bhavati---yadi pañcaiva pramāṇavyavahārasādhanānyabhaviṣyan, yāvatā
śabdo'pi pramāṇavyavahārasādhanamiti । na punaḥ pramāṇasvarūpamevātra sādhyate,
yena pañcaśabdātpramāṇāntaramāpadyeta । nanvevaṃ kimiti vyākhyāyate ? yāvatā
pramāṇaśabdaḥ pramāṇasvarūpapara evāstu; pramāṇavyavahārasādhanābhiprāyeṇa mā
vyākhyāyi; abhāvaśca pramāṇantaramabhyupagamyatām; tadāha---<q>pramāṇāntarābhyupagame
ko doṣa iti</q> । pariharati---<q>na khalu kaścit brahmahatyādiḥ</q>; kintvapramāṇaṃ
yat pramāṇameva na bhavati, tatpramāṇamityuktaṃ bhavati; uktena nyāyenābhāvasya
﻿<pb n="205"/>
pramāṇatā nāstīti tasya prāmāṇyamuktaṃ syādityasadaṅgīkāra eva doṣa iti ।
lakṣaṇagranthaśca bhāṣyakārīyo'nādṛto bhavati---pramāṇābhāvo'bhāvaḥ---ityevaṃrūpaḥ ।
<q>anapekṣatvaṃ ca sarvapramāṇānāṃ nirastaṃ bhavati</q> । abhāvasya pratyakṣādi-
sāpekṣasyāpi pramāṇatvopagame aparamapi pramāṇaṃ sāpekṣamityāśaṅkyeta । tasmāt
pramāṇāntarābhāvāt vyavahārasādhanābhiprāya evāyaṃ pañcaśabdaḥ kṛtaḥ ।
<q>upasaṃharati---tasmātsiddhaṃ viṣayāntaraṃ śabdasya</q> । pratyakṣādiviṣayādviṣayāntaraṃ
śabdasya siddham, nirapekṣakāryapratipādakatvāt । <q>tatsiddhau ca prāmāṇyasiddhiḥ</q> ।
yadi śabdaprāmāṇyasiddhirevātra prakṛtā kartavyā, tadā <q>kimarthaṃ tarhi pañcagraha-
ṇam</q> ? evaṃ vaktavyam---yadi catvārīti । yadi vyavahārasādhanatāmātraṃ śabdasya
sādhyaṃ syāt, tadā tāvadidaṃ yuktam; yadā tu prāmāṇyamapi sādhyameva, tadā pañca-
grahaṇena kim ? pariharati---<q>vyavahārapañcakapradarśanārtham</q> । śabdavyavahārāti-
riktavyavahārapañcakaṃ darśayituṃ pañcagrahaṇam । <q>pañcagrahaṇe hyakriyamāṇe vyavahārāntaraṃ
pradarśitaṃ na syāt</q> । yata eva vyavahārāntarabuddhiḥ prayatnasādhyā na sukhena
saṃbhavati, <q>ata evāphalavatī śākheti pratyakṣajameva vyavahāraṃ manyante ।</q>
naiyāyikāḥ । nanu yadi manyante, manyantāṃ tarhi; tatrāha---<q>pramāṇaviṣayā</q>-
﻿<pb n="206"/>
<q>vacchedajaścāyaṃ vyavahāraḥ</q> । <quote>‘ayameva’</quote> iti pramāṇaviṣayamavacchidya sādhyavadhāraṇa-
jñānena niścityābhāvavyavahāraḥ pravartate । nanvevaṃ tarhyavacchedakatve pramāṇāntaramā-
padyeta, tatrāha---<q>na ca pramāṇaviṣayāvacchedo viṣayāntaratayā śakyate vaktum</q> ।
yadā dṛśye'pi vastvantare svarūpamātropalabdhirbhavati, tadā vastvantarasya
nāstitvamiti pramāṇasvarūpavimarśa evāvacchedaḥ; na punarvastutaḥ svarūpāntaram ।
ato na pramāṇāntarāpattiḥ । kathaṃ punaḥ pramāṇaviṣayāvacchedajo'yaṃ vyavahāraḥ
viṣayasvarūpāvagamādeva kimiti na bhavati ? tatrāha---<q>na ca viṣayamātrāvagamā-
tpūrvapramāṇānāmavacchedādṛte nāstīti vyavahāro'vakalpate</q> । <quote>‘nāsti’</quote> iti
śabdaprayogātmako niśśaṅkagamanalakṣaṇaśca vyavahāro na svarūpamātrāvagamādeva bhavati ।
<q>tasmāt siddhaṃ vyavahārānyatvam</q> । pañca vyavahārāḥ svarūpāvagamanibandhanāḥ;
eko vyavahāro'vacchedanibandhanaḥ । yata eva vyavahāramātravarijñānāyedamuktam, na
punarabhāvākhyapramāṇasvarūpanirūpaṇāya, ata eva vyavahārāntarasidhyarthaṃ <q>vyavahāra-
kāla eva pañcasaṅkhyopanyāsaḥ; na pramāṇasvarūpābhidhānakāle ṣaṭsaṃkhyo-
﻿<pb n="207"/>
panyāsaḥ । tasmādatraiva pañcisaṅkhyopanyāsādavaitu bhavān---abhāvavyava-
hārasyeyaṃ bhedikā pañcasaṅkhyā, na svarūpasya</q> । yadi hi svarūpasya bhedo'-
bhimataḥ syāt, pramāṇābhidhānakāla eva ṣaṭsaṃkhyopanyasyetaḥ tena vyavahāra-
kāle pañcasaṃkhyopādānādavagaccha---vyavahāramātra eva bheda iti । <q>prasiddhistu
dattottarā</q> । vaṭayakṣaprasiddhitulyatābhidhānena ṣaṭpramāṇaprasiddhirnirmūletyuktam ।।</p>
<p>iti citrādiparihāraḥ</p>
<p><q><quote>“yattu pratyakṣaviruddhaṃ vacanamupanyastam---<quote>“sa eṣa yajñāyudhī
yajamānaḥ”</quote> iti pratyakṣaṃ śarīrakaṃ vyapadiśati iti”</quote>---atrāpi śarīrakamitya-
siddham । kastarhi vyapadiśyate ? yasyaitaccharīram</q> । sa vyapadiśyata ātmā ।
<q>nanu <quote>“eṣaḥ”</quote> iti vyapadeśaḥ, na <quote>‘yasyaiṣaḥ’</quote> iti</q> yadi hi <quote>‘yasyaiṣa kāyaḥ, sa
yajñāyudhī yajamāno'ñjasā svargaṃ lokaṃ yati’</quote> iti vyapadeśaḥ, tadā yāvadātmābhi-
﻿<pb n="208"/>
prāyeṇāpi yajñāyudhīvyapadeśo ghaṭeta; yadā tu <quote>‘eṣaḥ’</quote> iti yajñāyudhina eva
sāmānādhikaraṇyena vyapadeśaḥ, tadātmano'nyapuruṣāpratyakṣatvānnopapannamidamātmābhiprā-
yeṇāpi; tatra eṣaśabdānuguṇyādyajñāyudhīti śarīrakameva vācyam, tatra spaṣṭaḥ
pratyakṣavirodhaḥ । <q>uttaram--- abhedopacāranibandhano'yaṃ vyapadeśaḥ---mañcāḥ krośa-
ntītivat</q> । asyārthaḥ---etacchabdena vak‍tṛpratyakṣo'rtho'bhidhīyate; yacca pratyakṣaṃ
tadapi spaṣṭasattvam, ātmā aspaṣṭasadbhāva iti sa gauṇyā vṛttyocyate <quote>‘eṣaḥ’</quote> iti ।
abhedopacāraśabdena gauṇī vṛttiruktā । paraśabdena paro vyapadiśyata ityatra dṛṣṭānto
mañcāḥ krośantīti । lakṣaṇā tveṣā tātsthyena । <q>kimityaupacārikaḥ śabdārtho
gṛhyate</q> ? uttaram---<q>tathāvagateḥ</q> । anvitābhidhānavyutpatteranvayayogyārthopasthāpakatayā
tathāvagateḥ gauṇatvāvagateḥ; na hi śarīraṃ svargagamanayogyam । <q>uktamartha-
vādapadānāmanyaparatvāt gauṇyevāvagatiḥ</q> । iti śabdaścātra draṣṭavyaḥ । <q>nanu
cānyatvopalabdhau satyāṃ gorvāhīkasya ca gauṇo nirdeśaḥ upapadyate</q>
﻿<pb n="209"/>
govāhīkayorbhedopalabdhau satyāṃ mukhyatvānupapattyā <q>gauṇo nirdeśa upapadyate
<quote>‘gaurvāhīkaḥ’</quote> iti । na cātra śarīrādanyamupalabhāmahe</q> । yo gauṇyā vṛttyā
vyapadiśyate । <q>nopalabhāmaha iti ko'bhiprāyaḥ</q> ? upalabhyata eveti matvā
pṛcchati । uttaram---<q>ayamevābhiprāyo nopalabhāmaha iti । nanu ca kārya-
bhūtaiḥ prāṇādibhirena1mupalabhāmahe</q> । kādācitkaṃ kāryaṃ samavāyikāraṇamanu-
māpayati; tenānumānenātmā pratīyate । <q>nanu śarīrameva prāṇityapāniti
ca</q> । pratyakṣaśarīrakāraṇasadbhāve na kāraṇāntarānumānamupapadyata iti bhāvaḥ ।

<q>anumānāt pratyakṣaṃ balīya iti naiyāyikāḥ</q> । tena pratyabhijñābalenābhi-
vyañjakavaidharmyānumānaṃ bādhyata iti । <q>nanu pratyakṣaṃ bhramabhāk</q> । ataḥ kathaṃ balīya
iti । <q>anumāne'pi bhrāntiraviśiṣṭā</q> । anu1māne'pi bhrāntiviśeṣamāha---<q>na brūmaḥ
anumāne bhrāntirnāstīti ; kintvatra bhedāgrahaṇāttadba‍uddhiratasminna2pi bhavati</q> ।
jvālādivaditi । saṃbhāvitabhramamitipratyakṣameva durbalamiti manyāmahe । <q>anayaiva
prakaṭitāprakaṭitabhramakāraṇatayoktaṃ nyāyavidbhiḥ-<quote>“bhavati vai pratyakṣādapyanumānaṃ
balīyaḥ”</quote> iti</q> । idānīṃ rāddhāntacchāyayā pṛcchati---<q>kiṃ nirjñātakāraṇaduṣṭatai-
vātropanyastā ?</q> nirjñātā cāsau kāraṇaduṣṭatā ceti । pūrvapakṣyāha---<q>kiṃ jātaṃ
yadyupanyastāṃ ?</q> yajjātaṃ tadāha---<q>nanu ca viparyayā/?/bhāvānnaivāstitayāpenya</q>-
<note>1. anumānamapi bhrāntamasti. viśeṣamāha. ga.</note>
<note>2. atasminnasti. ga.</note>
﻿<pb n="281"/>
<q>situṃ śakyate</q> । na hi sākṣāt bhedajñānaṃ śabde vidyate, yena viparyayo bhavet ।
pūrvapakṣī pṛcchati---<q>kiṃ viparyaya eva mithyātve hetuḥ</q> ? ekagranthenāha---
yāvatā <q>kāraṇadoṣo'pyasamīcīnahetutayopanyasta eva</q> । tena viparyayābhāve'pi
kāraṇadoṣānmithyātvaṃ bha1vati । <q>nanu ca kāraṇadoṣaḥ prayatnenopalabhyamāna-
tayoktaḥ</q> । pūrvapakṣyāha---<q>ko'yaṃ prayatno nāma, yo'sāvatra nāstītyucyate ?
ayamevāsau prayatnaḥ---anyatra viparyayātkāraṇadoṣaṃ vijñāya tadbhāvabhāvitayaiva
<quote>‘etatkṛto'yaṃ viparyayaḥ’</quote> iti tamanyatra vijānāti; jñāte ca tasmi-
nnasatyapi viparyaye <quote>‘bhrāntamidam’</quote> ityadhyavasyati । kimatraivaṃbhūtamasti</q> ?
ityekagranthaḥ । bādhakapratyaye hi jāte mithyābhāve'vagate sati kiṃ-
nibandhanamidaṃ mithyātvamiti jijñāsamānaḥ kāraṇadoṣatadbhāvabhāvitayā tasyaiva
tatra kāraṇatāṃ niścinoti; niścite ca tasmin yatrāpi bādhakapratyayo
nāsti, tatrāpi mithyātvahetukāraṇadoṣajñānena mithyātvamadhyavasyati; tadevaṃvidhaṃ
kimatrāsti ? yāvatā nāstyeva, bādhakasya kadācidapyadarśanāditi । pūrvapakṣyāha
---bāḍhamatiśayenāsti bhedāgrahaṇam; <q>bhedāgrahaṇanibandhana eva śuktikādiṣu
rajatabhramaḥ; evamatrāpi bhedāgrahaṇanibandhana eva jvālādiṣviva ta2dbhramaḥ</q> ।
śuktikārajatādiṣu sākṣādbādhakodaye sati bhedāgrahaṇasya mithyātvahetubhāve'vagate
<note>1. bhaviṣyati. ga.</note>
<note>2. tad‍grahaḥ. ka.</note>
﻿<pb n="282"/>
śabde bādhakābhāve'pi bhedāgrahaṇanibandhanastadga‍ho bhaviṣyatīti । <q>tasmāt suṣṭhūktaṃ
śabda eva ta1d‍grahaṇaṃ bhrāntiriti</q> । pūrvapakṣyevāha---<q>yasya tāvadviparītākāramarthe
jñānamutpadyate kadācit, tasya yuktaṃ vak‍tum <quote>‘viparyayābhāvānnāyaṃ bhramaḥ’</quote>
iti</q> । viparītakhyātipakṣe gṛhītameva nāstīti khyāpanīyam; tatra viparītākāra-
paricchinne vastunyanumānaṃ na kramata iti pratyakṣāntareṇa yadi mithyātvaṃ syāt,
syādapi । <q>yasya punaragrahaṇanibandhana eva vipa2ryayaḥ, tasya punaḥ kā śakti-
rvak‍tumanumānavirodhe sati jvālādivaiṣamyam</q> ? na hi tasya mate gṛhītasya
mithyātvaṃ khyāpyate, kiṃ tvagṛhītabhedo gṛhyate ityavirodhenānumānamutpadyata
eva yathā jvālādiṣviti । <q>nanu cāgrahaṇamapi punargrahaṇādavasīyate ।
na cātra kasyāṃcidavasthāyāṃ bhedasya grahaṇamasti saugandhikasphaṭika-
yoriva</q> । uparāgopadhānena sphaṭikaḥ padmarāgaviśeṣātsaugandhikādbhedena na gṛhyate,
uparāgāpagame tu gṛhyate; tatheha nāsti; tasmātkathaṃ bhedāgrahaṇametaditi
kalpyate ? pūrvapakṣyāha---<q>jvālādiṣu katham</q> ? tatrāpi bhedagrahaḥ pratyakṣeṇa
nāstītyarthaḥ । <q>anumānādbhedāvagatiriti cet</q>, tulyamatrānumānamityuktam ।
upasaṃharati---<q>tasmācchabdaviṣayaṃ sapratyabhijñaṃ pratyakṣamāśāpāśanibandhanaṃ mīmāṃ</q>-
<note>1. Omitted. tad‍grahaṇa. ka.</note>
<note>2. mithyātvam. ka.</note>
﻿<pb n="283"/>
<q>sakānāmiti । yadapyuktamanyaiḥ---tulye'pi saṃskārye saṃskārabhedāt
kāryānyatvamupalabhyata iti yathā maṇḍūkavasayāktākṣā vaṃśānuragāniva
paśyantīti</q> । anenedamuktama---yadyapyekameva śrotraṃ saṃskāryam, tathāpi
saṃskārabhedāt kadācitkiñcideva śabdaṃ viṣayaprāptaṃ grahīṣyati; yathaikameva
cakṣurmaṇḍūkavasāñjanalakṣaṇasaṃskārabhedāt kiñcideva rūpaṃ gṛhṇātīti ।
dūṣayati---<q>tadapyāśāpāśavijṛmbhitam; saṃskāro hi nāma sa bhavati,
yaḥ svakārye śaktimupajanayati; na caitadindriyasya kāryam, yadidama1yathārtha-
grahaṇam; agrahaṇameva taditi pratipāditam</q> । na maṇḍūkavasāñjanaṃ
netrasaṃskāraḥ, kintu śaktipratibandhakameva; ata eva vaṃśākārasyāpratītiḥ,
uragākārasya smaraṇamiti smṛtipramoṣe darśitam । <q>tasmādabhede'pi saṃskāryasya
saṃskārānyatvena kāryānyatvaṃ kvacidapi jñāpake na vidyate ityanyat
kiñci2dudāharaṇamupadarśanīyam</q> । na ca tacchakyate । <q>yacca khaṅgadarpaṇādi-
ṣvanyathābhivyajyate mukhamiti, kimuktaṃ bhavati</q> ? abhivyañjakabhedāt
kiṃ bhedena pratīyate yathā darpaṇe'bhivyañjake'nyadrūpaṃ mukhasya dṛśyate, khaṅge
cānyaditi ? dūṣayati---<q>grāhye'yamuparāgo dṛṣṭaḥ</q> । asyārthaḥ---tatrāpi
na vyañjakabhedena grahaṇam, kintvekameva mukhaṃ gṛhyate; grāhyaṃ tvabhivyañjaka-
<note>1. anyathārtha. ga.</note>
<note>2. -dudāharaṇīyam. ka, ga.</note>
﻿<pb n="284"/>
bhūtadarpaṇādyanuraktamiti tadvaśenānyadiva bhāti । yuktaścāyamuparāgaḥ, abhi-
vyañjakasyāpi viṣayatvāt; <q>iha punaḥ śrotramagrāhyam</q>, yena tadanurāgeṇa pratītiḥ
syāt; saṃyogavibhāgāvapyagrāhyau; tena tadvaśenāpi bhedapratītirnāsti ।
<q>tasmādidamapyāśāpāśavijṛmbhitameva</q> । tasmācchabdo nitya iti śraddhayaiva
pramāṇaśūnyatayā pratipattavyam । kasmācchraddhayaiva pratipattavyamityāśaṅkyāha---
<q>śabdātmakatvādvedasya vedanindā mā bhūditi</q> । śabde'nitye śabdātmako
vedo'pyanitya ityaṅgīkaraṇīyam । anityatvanindāyāṃ doṣamāha---<q>paṭhitaṃ ca
dharmaśāstrakāraiḥ---<quote>“sa sādhubhirbahiṣkāryo nāstiko vedanindakaḥ”</quote>
iti</q> । yata eva nityatā śabdasya vak‍tuṃ na śakyate, tasmādanidaṃprathama-
taivātra vedavyavahāre śaraṇam; aparibhāvitatattvairaparān vyavaharato dṛṣṭvā । vedasya
vyavahāraḥ pravartyate; tairapyaparavyahāradarśanāt tairapyevamiti ayaṃ prathama iti
nāsti, anāditvāt saṃsārasya । na punaḥ śabdanityatāpūrvakaṃ vedasya
prāmāṇye'napekṣatvaṃ śakyate yuktito vak‍tum । yadi punarandhaparamparātulya-
tvādanidaṃprathamatayā loko na vyavaharati, tarhi lokaḥ kalpyatāṃ vā
rāgādivinirmuktamāśayadoṣarahitaṃ yathādṛṣṭārthavādinaṃ rāgādivinirmuktatve'pyupa-
deśasiddhaye karuṇāviṣṭacetasaṃ rāgādivirahe'pi karuṇayā rāgādivyatiriktayā
parahitabuddha‍yā svārthanirapekṣayāviṣṭacittatvāt parebhya upadeśasya dātāramaprati-
hatajñānaṃ bhagavantaṃ kañcana munivaraṃ dharmātiśayasaṃpannaṃ dharmabalenaivāpratihata-
﻿<pb n="285"/>
jñānam । yathāhuḥ---<quote>“ārṣaṃ siddhadarśanaṃ ca dharmebhyaḥ”</quote> iti । yāvaddha‍yevaṃvidhaḥ
puruṣo lokairna kalpitaḥ, tāvattadvacanabhūtādvedādarthaniścayapūrvako vyavahāro
lokasya na sidhyati । kalpyatāmiti ṇyantād‍‍dvitīyo ṇic; lokaḥ kalpayaṃ-
stvayā vedavyavahārasamarthanavādinā prayujyatāmiti । atha vedārthasya sakala-
pramāṇāviṣayatvāttadvidhaṃ puruṣaṃ lokaḥ kalpayituṃ na śaknoti, tadā---<q>āśrīyatāṃ
vā suragurordarśanam</q> । saṃvyavahāramevedamadṛṣṭaprayojanarahitaṃ vedatrayābhihitamarthaṃ
prājñairlokayātrāsiddha‍yarthaṃ svakīyāṃ bhojanaśayanādilokayātrāṃ sādhayituṃ supratibandhaṃ
suprayuktaṃ ḍambhātmakamanupālyamānaṃ paśyāma iti । yadāhuḥ---</p>
<lg><l><quote>“agnihotraṃ trayo vedāstridaṇḍaṃ (puṇḍraṃ) bhasmaguṇṭhanam ।</l>
<l>buddhipauruṣahīnānāṃ jīviketi bṛhaspatiḥ ।।”</quote> iti ।
<p>idameva suragurordarśanaṃ yuktaṃ manyāmahe; na hi dṛṣṭe lokayātrā-
siddha‍yarthatve satyadṛṣṭakalpanā nyāyyā; tena yadidamucyate---yadyayamapramāṇabhūtaḥ
pauruṣeya eva vedaḥ, kimiti traivarṇikānāṃ mahatāṃ mahatā prayatnena
vedādhyayanadhāraṇatadarthānuṣṭhānalakṣaṇo vyavahāra iti, tadanyathāsiddhaṃ
kṛtam ; ṛjubhyo ḍambhena jīvikālābhena prayāsasyārthavattvāt ।
<q>dṛṣṭaścāyamarthaḥ prājñaiḥ ṛjava upajīvyanta iti । yathāprasiddhamāgamavādi-
nāmapi hetudarśanādaprāmāṇyam <quote>“yūpahastino dānamācaranti”</quote> ityeva-
mādiṣu</q> । asyārthaḥ---ye'pyāgamaṃ pramāṇamicchanti, te'pi <quote>“yūpahastino
dānamācaranti”</quote> ityevamādiṣu ṛtviggatalobhalakṣaṇahetudarśanādaprāmāṇyamāhuḥ ।
﻿<pb n="286"/>
tathā hi---kenacidṛtvijā lobhiṣṭhena śraddhāpradhāno yajamānaḥ kaścidyūpahastidānaṃ
kāritaḥ; taddarśanādeṣā smṛtiḥ kṛtā---ityādhārahetudarśanāt dṛḍhayorapi
smṛtyācārayoraprāmāṇyam; evamatrāpi jīvikālobhalakṣaṇahetudarśanādācārasya
na prāmāṇyamiti । athaitanneṣṭaṃ tadā kartavyo vā sapratyabhijñapratyakṣasya
śabdo viṣaya iti yatnaḥ । saṃprati samādhātāha---<q>kathaṃ punarjvālā-
derivānumānācchakyate'nyatvamavagantum</q> ? yathā jvālāderanumānādanyatvaṃ
śakyate'vagantum, tathā kathaṃ śabdasyānyatvaṃ śakyate'vagantum । ākṣeptāha
---<q>nanu cānumānādityuktam</q> । samādhātāha---<q>kiṃ tadanumānamiti</q> ।
ākṣeptāha---<q>abhivyañjakānāmanekaviṣayā śaktirdṛṣṭeti</q> । ye'bhivyañjakāsteṣā-
manekaviṣayā śaktiḥ, yathā dīpasya; abhivyañjakāśca saṃyogavibhāgā
bhavata iti । samādhātāha---<q>nanu cedamabhivyañjakaviṣayamanumānam</q> ।
anekaviṣayābhivyaktisādhakam । ekagranthenāha---kathamanyaviṣayamanumāna-
manyaviṣayasya śabdaviṣayasyānyatvasyāvacchittau hetuḥ ? punarapyekagranthenāha---
<q>śrotrasya hyabhivyañjakasaṃskāraṃ niruṇaddhi</q> । etadanumānam <quote>‘śrotramabhivyañjakena
saṃskriyate’</quote> ityetannirākaroti । <q>na punaḥ śabdasyānyatvamavagamayati</q> ।
ākṣeptāha---nanu coktam, na cetsaṃyogavibhāgāḥ śrotrasya saṃskāraṃ

﻿<pb n="287"/>
cānyatvamiti</q> । yadi saṃyogavibhāgāḥ śrotraṃ na saṃskuryuḥ, tadā śabdotpā-

nyasyotpattimavagamayati</q> ? śrotrasaṃskārasya pratiṣedhe kathamanyasya

kimanyadataḥ śabdotpatteḥ kuryuḥ ? samādhātāha---<q>kiṃ yasya saṃskārakatā

manyante</q> ? ākṣeptāha---<q>evaṃ manyante---na cecchrotre kāryamasti, śabde kāryaṃ

śabde tadgra/?/haṇāt । <quote>‘sa evāyaṃ śabdaḥ’</quote> iti śabdasya tatpratyayāt utpattistāvanna
kāryam, utpattau satyāmanyatvasyāvaśyaṃbhāvitvāt; sa iti pratyayavirodhāt;
na ca śabde'bhivyaktiḥ saṃbhavatīti । ubhayavādisaṃmatamākṣeptāha---yadi
śabdasyotpattiṃ na kurvanti, <q>kiṃ tarhi kurvanti saṃyogavibhāgāḥ</q> ? samādhātāha
---śrotrasaṃskāraṃ kurvantīti brūmaḥ । ākṣeptāha---nanu cānyairnayanonmī-
lanādibhirindriyasaṃskārakaiḥ samānadeśavartisakalarūpādyupalambhahetubhiḥ sahāmīṣāṃ
﻿<pb n="289"/>
saṃyogavibhāgānāṃ śrotrasaṃskārakatvenābhyupagatānāṃ pratiniyataśabdopalambhahetutārūpa-
vilakṣaṇatā nopapadyata ityuktam । samādhātāha---<q>anumānāt kāryābhāvaṃ
manyate bhavān; vayaṃ tu pratyakṣādutpattiṃ necchāmaḥ; pratyakṣānumānayośca
pratyakṣaṃ balīya iti siddham</q> । asyārthaḥ---śrotre kāryaṃ na bhavatītyabhi-
vyañjakasāmānyānumānāt bhavāt manyate, śrotre ca kāryābhāvamanumāne-
nāvagamya śabde tadgra/?/haṇabādhanīmutpattiṃ kalpayati; vayaṃ tu sapratyabhijñāt
pratyakṣāt śabdasyaikatāṃ pratipadyamānā utpattimanicchantaḥ śrotrasaṃskāra-
mabhivyañjakasāmānyānumānaprasaktasakalopalambhabādhena niyataśabdaviṣayaṃ kalpayāmaḥ;
evaṃ ca tvadīyaṃ śabdotpattyanumānam anumānāntarapūrvakam; asmadīyaṃ
tu pratyakṣapūrvakaṃ niyataśabdaviṣayaśrotrābhivyaktikalpanam; pratyakṣānumānayośva
śīghrapravṛttatayā pratyakṣaṃ balīya iti sakalavādināṃ siddham; anumāne
tu sambandhavyāptigrahaṇasmaraṇapakṣadharmatādhyavasānalakṣaṇā sā1magrī bahutaravilamba-
saṃpā2danīyā; pratyakṣe tu nārthāntaraparigrahasavyapekṣā kā3cidastīti śīghratara-
pravṛttānumānavaśenaiva vastunirṇaya iti---yuktaṃ tadgra/?/haṇe sati niyataviṣayābhi-
vyaktijanakatvaṃ saṃyogavibhāgayoḥ । ākṣeptāha---<q>nanu cāgrahaṇaṃ bhramaheturityuktaṃ
jvālādīnāmiva</q> । asyārthaḥ---yadi tadgrahaṇamevedaṃ siddhaṃ syāt, tadā
tadbalabhāvyanumānaṃ balīyo bhavet; yāvatā yathā jvālādiṣu bhinneṣvapi
bhedāgraha4ṇamātrāttadgra/?/haṇaṃ bhramaḥ, tathā ayamapi tadgrahaṇabhrama eveti
kathametatpūrvakamanumānaṃ balīya iti । samādhātāha---<q>iha tvagrahaṇamevāsiddham</q> ।

nātra bhedāgrahaṇametaditi niścitam; tena pratītibalāttadgra/?/ha evāyamiti
siddhametatpūrvakasyānumānasya balīyastvam । ākṣeptā sāmyāpādanābhiprāyeṇāha---
tatra jvālādau kathamagrahaṇasiddhiriti । samādhātottaramāha---<q>kāryānumānāt</q> ।
prabhāvitatilakṣaṇāt kāryājjvālādiṣu bhedānumānāt bhedāgrahaṇaṃ siddham; iha tu
tadeva kāryaṃ bhedānumānahetubhūtamadyāpi na siddham । na cāsiddhaṃ śabde bhedāgrahaṇa-
siddhau paryāptaṃ bhavati । pratyakṣaṃ tvanapekṣatvāt siddham । ākṣeptāha---<q>anumāne vā
kāpekṣā</q> ? na kācidapekṣetyarthaḥ । samādhātāha---<q>iyamevāpekṣā---siddhe'numāne
kāryam</q> । nātra prabhātulyaṃ kāryaṃ pratyakṣasiddhamastītyanumānata eva kāryamavagantavyam;
ataḥ siddhe'numāne kāryaṃ vijñeyam; <q>kārye ca satyanumānam</q> । yadapi
tadanumānam, tadapi liṅgāpekṣamiti tasya kāryaṃ liṅgaṃ vaktavyam; ataḥ
kārye satyanumānena pravartitavyam; ato'numeyakāryāpekṣatvāt sāpekṣa-

tad‍grahaṇāpekṣam</q> । yathānumānaṃ bhedāgrahaṇāpekṣam, naivaṃ pratyakṣaṃ tadgra/?/haṇā-

saṃskārajanakāviti yuktam । <q>kuto'nyataḥ</q> ? śrotrārthatayā prasiddhau ।

śrūyata iti cet, naitadevam; na nūnamuparamanti saṃyogavibhāgāḥ, yata

﻿<pb n="293"/>

iti vacanaṃ naiva ghaṭate; ato vāyavīyābhiprāyeṇaiva parihāraḥ । ākṣipati---
yadyevaṃ spaṣṭīkṛtam, <q>idānīmuttaragrantho nopapadyate <quote>“ākāśaviṣayatvāttasya,

﻿<pb n="294"/>

naiva ghaṭate । <q>satyaṃ na ghaṭate</q> । ekagranthenāha---<q>kāryāntaropalabdhistu pratyakṣaiva,

abhivyaktyantaradarśanādabhivyañjakāntarakalpanopapanneti । pariharati---<q>na tulyam;
na hyabhivyaktirabhivyaktyantaramārabhate</q> । kvacidadarśanāt । <q>kāryasya tu kāryā-
ntarārambhe na kaścidvirodhaḥ3; bhavati hyāpekṣikaṃ kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca</q> ।
mūlakāraṇāpekṣayā kāryam, svakīyakāryāpekṣayā kāraṇaṃ ca । <q>na4 punarabhivyakti-
rabhivyañjikā ceti</q> । apamarthaḥ---nābhivyaktāvapi tulyam; yasmānnābhivyakti-
rabhivyaktyantaramārabhate kvacidapyadṛṣṭatvāt; kāryaṃ tu kāryāntaramārabhata eva,
loke prāyeṇa darśanāt । tenādyāḥ saṃyogavibhāgāḥ śabdamārabhante; tadārabdhāḥ

﻿<pb n="321"/>
kālāntarāvasthāyitvamuccāraṇakālatkālāntarāvasthāyitvaṃ nityaśabdenocyate; <q>na
sadakāraṇatvam</q> । nityaśabdena hi svaśak‍tyā sadakāraṇamucyate;
<quote>‘yatsadakāraṇaṃ tannityam’</quote> iti lokaprasiddham, yathā gaganamātmetyādi । yathāha
bhagavān kāśyapaḥ <quote>“sadakāraṇaṃ nityam”</quote> iti । tadidaṃ na nityaśabdenocyate;
api tu lakṣaṇayā kālāntarāvasthāyitvameva । atra codayati---<q>nanu
ca sannakāraṇaśca śabda iṣyate</q> । tena śrautameva nityatvaṃ nityaśabdena kimiti
nocyata iti bhāvaḥ । pariharati---<q>bāḍhamiṣyate; sa tu pārārthamātratayaiva
darśanasya sidhyati</q> । yadaiva hi kālāntarāvasthāyitvena śabdasyoccāraṇasya para-
pratipattyarthatā sthitā, na śabdakāraṇatā, tadaivaṃ sidhyatīti na prayatnena sādhyate ।
atra codayati---yadi hi tāvadiṣyate sadakāraṇatā śabdasya, kimiti
tarhi prayatnena nityaśabde'pyuccārite kālāntarāvasthāyitaiva sādhyata iti viśeṣa
ucyate; yāvatā nityataiva sādhyatām; na kālāntarāvasthāyiteti । pariharati
---<q>kathaṃ nāmānityasyāpi dhūmāderdṛṣṭāntatā syāditi</q> । yadi hi nityataiva
sādhyeta tadā dhūmādīnāṃ dṛṣṭāntatā na syāt, sādhyavikalatvāt;
dhūmādivyaktayo hi sāmānyenopādhinā agnisambandhavyāptā agnivyaktimeva
gamayanti । na ca dhūmādivyaktīnāṃ sadakāraṇatā, kintu kālāntarā-
vasthāyitā । tasmāt dṛṣṭāntalābhāya kālāntarāvasthāyitaiva sādhyā । aparaścodayati
---nanu cāsyāpi śabdasyānityatā prāpnoti, prasiddhe dhūmādau darśanāt ।
﻿<pb n="322"/>
yathābhūto hi dṛṣṭānte dharmo dṛṣṭaḥ, tathābhūtenaiva dārṣṭāntike'pi
bhavitavyam; tena dhūmavadanityatā śabdasya prāpnoti । pariharati---<q>ata
eva kālāntarāvasthāyitvamātraṃ sādhyatayocyate</q> । yata eva dṛṣṭānte'-
nityatā dṛśyate, ata eva kālāntarāvasthāyitvamātraṃ sādhyatayocyate;
anyathā dṛṣṭāntābhāvaprasaṅgāt । nanu bhavatu kālāntarāvasthāyitā,
nityatā tu tadvadeva na syādityatrāha---<q>kālāntarāvasthāyitayā ca siddhaṃ
sadakāraṇatvaṃ śabdasya</q> । tenānityatā na prasajyate । tadā kathaṃ sadakāraṇatā
sidhyatītyatrāha---<q>darśanameva hi tasya kāraṇatayā śaṅkitaṃ paraiḥ</q> ।
uccāraṇameva hi śabdasya kāraṇatayā śaṅkitam; tacca kālāntarāvasthāyitve
siddhe dvitīyaśravaṇe parārthatayā parapratipattyarthatayā akāraṇatāṃ śabdaṃ prati gatam,
kintu abhivyañjakameva; tataśca prathamaśravaṇe'pi tadabhivyañjakameveti siddha-
makāraṇatvam । upasaṃharati---tasmāt parārthadarśanasambandhimātrasya dhūmāderdṛṣṭāntatvaṃ
śabdasyāpi sadakāraṇatvaṃ siddham । atra codayati---<q>nanu ca tattulyopādāna-
mabhedamupādāya sidhyati pārārthyaṃ darśanasya</q> । asyārthaḥ---uccāritamātre hi
vinaṣṭe śabde parārthamuccāraṇaṃ na ghaṭate, saṅketitasya śabdasya punarvyavahāra-
kāle'sattvādasaṅketitasya cāpratipādakatvāt; yadā punaḥ saṅketite

śabde vinaṣṭe'pi tattulyo'paro yaḥ śabda utpadyate tatsādṛśyena vyāmūḍhā
abhedamupādāyārthaṃ pratipadyanta iti ghaṭate, tadā taddarśanasya parārthatāpi
sidhyatīti naikāntena kālāntarāvasthāyitāṃ śaknoti gamayitum । pariharati---
<q>satyaṃ sidhyati; kintu netthaṃbhūtatve pramāṇamasti</q> । asya tatpratyayasya
prātibhāsikastāvadbādhakapratyayo nāsti śuktikārajatādivat; ānumāniko'pi

iti na śakyate vak‍tumiti । prātibhāsikabādhābhāvamāha---na kasyacidapyā-
saṃsāraṃ jantoḥ <quote>‘pūrvoccaritasadṛśamuccārayāmi’</quote> ityuccārayituḥ <quote>‘tatsadṛśo'yam’</quote>
iti śroturvā vijñānotpādo dṛṣṭaḥ । anena <quote>“kasyacitkṛtrimo bhaviṣyati sambandha
iti cet taduktam”</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ vyākhyātam । bhāṣye coktaśabdena <quote>“yasya
ca duṣṭaṃ karaṇaṃ yatra ca mithyeti pratyayaḥ, sa evāsamīcīnaḥ pratyayo
nānyaḥ”</quote> ityuktam; tena kṛtrimasambandhaśabdābhedabhrameṇārthapratyayo na bhavatī-
tyuktaṃ bhavati । yata evāyamabhrāntastatpratyayaḥ, <q>ata eva cāviparītaṃ

<p>atra kecit codayanti---pratya2bhijñānarūpaṃ pratyakṣaṃ na bhavatīti,

samavāyī puruṣa eko viṣayāṇāmanubhavitā । sa ca pratibuddhapūrvānubhava-

smaraṇagrahaṇacchāyāvāhinā jñānena kālāntarāvasthāyi vastu gṛhṇāti । kevalā

dbodhe sati pratyabhijñā; na ca śabdo'gṛhītaḥ pratibuddhasaṃskāreṇa pratyabhi-

saṃbhāvyamānasya prayatnasya śabdābhivyañjakatvāt, dvitīyaśravaṇe pratyabhijñāya-
mānatvāt ; na hi sa eva prayatnastasyotpādako'bhivyañjakaśceti yujyate ।

prayatnena śabde kiñcijjanyate, api tu śrotre ; tasmiṃstu śrotravartini saṃskāre

﻿<pb n="362"/>
yathānumānādekatvaṃ na sidhyati, tathā tavāpyanyatvaṃ kathaṃ setsyati ? kāryaṃ hi
kāraṇamanumāpayati, na punarekatvamanyatvaṃ vā tasya1 spṛśati । sa evāha---
<q>ekatayā ca2 vinā kiṃ na sidhyati ?</q> tena yadyekatvamavagantumaśakyaṃ mā śāki;
avagatenāpi tena prayojanaṃ nāstīti । codayitāha---<q>idaṃ na sidhyati;
na hyupāyāḥ kalpitā bhavanti</q> । asati ca punarekatve nopāyāḥ kalpitā
bhavanti; tasmādekatvaṃ yatnato vācyama । <q>na caikatāvagatiranumānādyukteti
coditam</q> । asyārthaḥ---na mayā <quote>‘anyatvamanumānādavagamyate’</quote> iti coditam,
kintu <quote>‘ekatvaṃ kathamavagamyate’</quote> iti coditam; tena mamāyamupālambha eva
nopapadyate <quote>‘anyatvaṃ vā katham’</quote> iti । vaiyāka3raṇānusārī pariharati---<q>naiṣa doṣaḥ;
anumānāt pramāṇatvamavacchidya, tataḥ punaravayavairekatāṃ vetti <quote>‘śuklaḥ paṭaḥ’</quote>
ityevamādiṣu</q> । asyārthaḥ---kāryataḥ kāraṇamanumāya punarapi tasyaikatvaṃ
vinā kāryānupapatteravayavaiḥ sahaikatāṃ vijānāti; yāvatā hi vinā kāryaṃ
nopapadyate, tāvadavakalpayati । tadidaṃ kāryānumānagamyamekatvamāgamādvyākaraṇāt
pratipannam । kīdṛśaḥ punarayamāgamārtha ityatrāha---<q>pratyastamitāśeṣāgamavikalpaṃ
svayaṃ brahma prakāśata iti</q> । pratyastamitā aśeṣā āgamavikalpā vyākaraṇa-
nibandhanāḥ prakṛtyādivikalpā yasminnityarthaḥ । <q>ya4ducyate <quote>“śrotragrahaṇe hyarthe
loke śabdaśabda prasiddhaḥ”</quote> iti, tadapyāgamaviruddham</q> । lokavyapadeśa-
viruddhamityarthaḥ. । tatrāha---<q>gauriti śabdo gauriti cārtho gauriti</q>

<q>ca jñānam</q> । kutaḥ ? <q>ekābhidhānanirdeśāt; na hi bhinnasya yugapadekābhidhānaṃ

ghātāḥ khalvapyete”</quote> iti ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="382"/>
<p><quote>“tadbha‍ūtānāṃ kriyārthena samāmnāyo'rthasya tannimittatvāt”</quote> iti sūtraṃ paṭhitvā
vyācaṣṭe---atrocyate । syādanupāyatvaṃ vedārthe vṛddhavyavahārasya, yadyarthānyatvaṃ

yānyeva loke padāni tānyeva vede'pi; ye ca loke padārthāsta eva
vede'pi; ataḥ kathamarthānyatvam ? atra codayati---<q>kimidaṃ pratyuktaṃ
punarucyate ?</q> kathaṃ pratyuktaṃ punarucyate ? kathaṃ pratyuktamityatrāha---
<q>parasparānvayo hi padārthānāṃ vākyārtha ityuktam</q> । na padārthamātraṃ vākyārthaḥ ।
kiṃ tarhi ? anvayaḥ । tasmātpadapadārthapratyabhijñānaṃ nānvaye hetuḥ । kāmaṃ
padaiḥ padārthamātramavabodhyatām; anvayasya kimāyātam ? nanu cānvayo lākṣaṇiko
bhavatu; padaṃ hi padārthamātre vyutpannaṃ padārthamātraṃ bodhayiṣyati; sa ca
padārtho'nvayamātmano lakṣayati; tenānvayaḥ śābdo bhaviṣyati । tatrāha---
﻿<pb n="383"/>
<q>pramāṇāntaraṃ ca nāstyasmin prayuktamityuktam</q> । lakṣaṇā hi jñāte tātparye
bhavati; na ca <quote>‘anvaye prayuktametatpadam’</quote> ityatrāṃśe pramāṇamasti । nanvānartha-
kyamevānanvaye, tenānvayaparateti । tadayuktam; vedenārthavatā bhavitavyamiti
pramāṇābhāvāt । api ca anvaye lakṣyamāṇe'pi ko'nvayaḥ kena padārthena
lakṣyatāmityatrāpi nāsti pramāṇam । ataḥ pramāṇaśūnyo vaidiko'nvayo nirbījaḥ ।
atrāha rāddhāntī---<q>padapadārthānabhijño mātṛpriyo bhavān</q> । yo mātṛ-
snehānubandhena gurukule na ciramuṣitaḥ । <q>kathamanabhijñaḥ ?</q> uttaramāha---<q>padārthā-
stāvannāvyatiṣaktāḥ kvacidupalabhyante, antato'styarthena</q> । vyatiṣaṅgo'nyonya-
sambandhaḥ, tadvanto'nyonyasambaddhāḥ sarvāvasthāsu padārthā upalabhyante ।
yatrāpyarthāntaraṃ nāsti, tatrāpyantato'styarthena vyatiṣaktāḥ । yadi vastusvabhāvataḥ
padārthāntaravyatiṣaktāḥ, <q>tataḥ kim ?</q> na hi tāvatā śabdena vyatiṣaktā
evābhidhātavyā iti bhāvaḥ । uttaram---<q>idaṃ tataḥ</q> । vyatiṣiktā evābhidheyā
iti । kutaḥ ? <q>tatpratipattaye hi śabdārthavyavahāraḥ</q> । yataḥ tathāvasthitameva vastu

﻿<pb n="399"/>
nimittaṃ na bhavati’</quote> iti kalpanāgranthe । <quote>“api ca prātipadikāduccarantī

﻿<pb n="400"/>
<p>nanu yadyatīndriyakāryābhidhāyino liṅādayaḥ, tadanvitasvārthābhidhāyīni
ca padāni, kathaṃ tarhi loke tadvyatirekeṇa śabdaprayoga ityatrāha---<q>loke
punaḥ pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayatayā yuktaiva, tatpūrvakatvācchabdavyavahārasya</q> ।
yadeva hi pramāṇāntareṇa pramīyate, tadeva loko vivakṣati; tenātīndriyakāryaṃ
parityajya kriyākāryatva eva śabdaṃ prayuṅkte lakṣaṇayā; apūrvakāryatā hi kriyākārya-
tvāvyabhicāriṇī; tena tatparatayā loko liṅādikaṃ prayuṅkte; padāntarāṇyapi
kāryānvitatayaiva prayujyanta iti na laukikaprayogavirodhaḥ । <q><quote>“tasmātpadebhya
eva padārthapratyayaḥ, padārthobhyo vākyārthapratyayaḥ”</quote> iti</q> bhāṣyam; tadanupapannam,
<quote>“padārthā eva vākyārthaḥ”</quote> iti darśitatvādityāśaṅkyāha---<q>vyākhyātamiti</q> ।
vyatiṣaṅgābhiprāyamiti pūrvameva vyākhyātam । upasaṃharati---<q>tasmādupapannaṃ</q>
﻿<pb n="401"/>
<q>vṛddhavyavahāranimittamautpattikatvaṃ sambandhasya, vedavākyārthapratipattihetutvaṃ
ca</q> । upapannaṃ tasya । vilambate ityādayastu śabdapratyabhijñāmātratayā pratyuktāḥ;
<q>abhidhāne hi sa doṣaḥ</q> । <quote>‘vilambate’</quote> <quote>‘pralambate’</quote> ityupasargatā vi-pra-śabdayoḥ, vipra
ityatra nāmatā svarūpābhede nopapadyata iti yaduktaṃ vaiyākaraṇaiḥ, tatpratyuktam; svarūpā-
bhede'pyabhidhānarūpatā bhinnaiva; tena kvacidanyārthatā na doṣaḥ । <q>samāsādīnāṃ
tu tatra tatra parihāro'bhidhīyate</q> । yadidamuktam---samāse padadvayasambandho
na bhavati rājapuruṣasya hastinaḥ ityādi, tasyāpi parihārastatra tatrābhidhīyate;
tena so'pi na doṣaḥ ।।</p>
<p><q><quote>“vedāṃścaike sannikarṣaṃ puruṣākhyāḥ”</quote></q> atra bhāṣyam <quote>“padavākyāśraya
ākṣepaḥ parihṛtaḥ”</quote> iti। tatreyamāśaṅkā---nanu kimidaṃ padaṃ vākyamiti ? yāvatā na
padavyatiriktaṃ vākyaṃ nāmāsti । ataḥ kathaṃ pṛthagupanyāsa ityāśaṅkyāha---<q>vibhāgā-
bhidhānādavibhaktakāryatvācca vivekaḥ</q> । vibhāgena padānāmabhidhāyakatvāt padavyava-
﻿<pb n="402"/>
hāraḥ; avibhaktaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ padānāmekaṃ kāryaṃ viśiṣṭaikārthapratipattiriti tannibandhana-
steṣveva padeṣu vākyavyavahāraḥ । tena kāryavaśena padavyavahāro varṇānām,
kāryavaśena ca vākyabhāvaḥ padānāmiti yukto vākyapadayorvivekaḥ । yaduktam
<quote>‘asmaraṇātkartuḥ akṛtako vedaḥ’</quote> iti, tadviruddhaṃ samākhyayā । kāṭhakamityādikā yā
samākhyā, sā kṛtakatāṃ vedasya darśayati । atra pṛcchati---<q>kiṃ kāryanibandha-
naiva samākhyā ?</q> ayamāśayaḥ---yadi kāryanibandhanaiva samākhyā syāt,
tadā samākhyayā kṛtakatvaṃ bhavet; yāvatā pravacanādapi samākhyā ghaṭata
eveti । uttaram---<q>bāḍham</q> । atiśayena karaṇanibandhanaiva samākhyā । kutaḥ ?
<q>asādhāraṇena hi vyapadeśo bhavati</q> । karaṇaṃ hyasādhāraṇam; na
hyekena kṛtasyāpareṇa karaṇaṃ saṃbhavati । <q>sādhāraṇaṃ ca pravak‍tṛtvam</q> ।
﻿<pb n="403"/>
bahavo'pi  pravaktāro bhavanti । yadi pravak‍tṛtvena vyapadeśo na bhavati,
<q>kathaṃ tarhi <quote>“kṛte granthe”</quote>, <quote>“tena proktam”</quote> iti ca sūtradvayaṃ
bhagavataḥ ?</q> uttaram---<q>proktavacanamayuktam, <quote>“samarthānām”</quote> iti virodhāt</q> ।
<quote>“samarthānāṃ prathamādvā”</quote> iti sāmarthye sati taddhito bhavati । na ca <quote>‘kaṭhena proktam’</quote>
ityasya vigrahavākyasya yo'rthaḥ, sa kāṭhakaśabdādavagamyate; tena sāmarthyā-
bhāvāttasminnarthe taddhito notpadyata eva; tenedaṃ vacanamayuktam । tasmāt samākhyā-
darśanāt kāryataiva vedasyāvagamyata iti ।।</p>
<p>atra codayati---<q>keyaṃ kāryatā nityatvācchabdānām, autpattikatvācca
sambandhasya ?</q> śabdāstāvanna kriyante, nityatvāt । na ca teṣāmarthasambandho'pi
kriyate, nityatvādeva । tasmāt keyaṃ kāryatā ? pari<q>harati---pramāṇāntarā-
pekṣitā</q> । asyārthaḥ---<quote>‘pramāṇāntareṇa ayamartho'nena pratipannaḥ’</quote> iti yeyaṃ
pramāṇāntarāpekṣitā, sā kṛtakatā । tathā ca kṛtakatvānurūpaṃ vedavaco dṛśyate---
﻿<pb n="404"/>
<quote>“babaraḥ prāvāhaṇiḥ”</quote> ityevamādi । pravāhaṇasyāpatyaṃ kīrtyate vede; tena
prāvāhaṇijanmanaḥ prāgayaṃ grantho nāstīti jñāyate । atrocyate---syādetadevam,
yadyanyathā karaṇamantareṇa asādhāraṇavyapadeśo nopapadyate; <q>prakarṣādapi hyasādhāraṇa-
vyapadeśo loke dṛṣṭaḥ</q> । vacana eva yaḥ prakarṣaḥ so'sādhāraṇa iti
tannibandhano'pi vyapadeśo ghaṭata eva । yathā bādarāyaṇena vedasya prāmāṇyaṃ
samākhyāyate । yata eva prakarṣādapi vyapadeśo ghaṭate, <q>ata eva sūtradvayapraṇayanaṃ
bhagavataḥ pāṇineḥ</q> । <quote>“kṛte granthe,”</quote> <quote>“tena proktam”</quote> iti ca ।
<quote>“samarthānām”</quote> ityasya cāvirodhaḥ, vacanaprakarṣe'pi sāmarthyasaṃbhavāt ।</p>
﻿<pb n="405"/>
<p><q>yaduktam <quote>“babaraḥ prāvāhaṇiḥ”</quote> iti</q> tatrocyate---<q>sthite prāmāṇya
guṇavādaṃ vakṣyati</q> । tena nyāyena varṇanīyametadityarthaḥ । nanvetat vakṣyamāṇaṃ
kimarthamuktaṃ tatrāha---<q>vakṣyamāṇameva ca bhāṣyakāreṇātra vyākhyātam</q> ।
codayati---<q>kimartham, <quote>‘vakṣyāmaḥ’</quote> iti noktaṃ ca ?</q> pariharati---<q>asambaddhato-
panyāsārtham</q> । atha kathamayamunmattoktisadṛśo na bhavatīti imāmasambaddhatā-
﻿<pb n="406"/>
mupanyasituṃ guṇavādenātra vyākhyātam । tāmasambaddhatāṃ pariharati---<q>na
śakyate jyotiṣṭomādiṣu vidhyuddeśeṣu kalpayituṃ tat; ekavākyatayā
ca <quote>“vanaspatayaḥ satramāsata”</quote> ityevamādīnām</q> । asambaddhatā nāstīti</p> ।
﻿<pb n="407"/>
<quote>“api ca avigītaḥ suhṛdupadeśaḥ”</quote> iti bhāṣyaṃ vyācaṣṭe---<q>sārvajanīna-
maviparyayaṃ darśayati</q> । na vedārthe kasyacidviparyayo'stītyarthaḥ । <q>tasmā-
ccodanaiva pramāṇaṃ dharmasyeti siddhaḥ pratijñātārthaḥ</q> ।।</p>
<p>iti śā1limiśrakṛtāyāmṛjuvimalāyāṃ pañcikāyāṃ</p>
<p>prathamasyādhyāyasya</p>
<p>prathamaḥ pādaḥ</p>
<p>samāptaḥ</p>
<note>1. Added. śrī. ka.</note>
